the Companies Act\n2006.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>Our audit work has been undertaken\nso that we might<a></a> state to the company's members those\nmatters we are required to state to them in an<a></a> auditor's\nreport and for no other purpose.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>To the\nfullest extent permitted by law, we do<a></a> not accept or assume\nresponsibility to anyone other than the company and the company's<a></a> members, as a body, for our audit work, for this report, or\nfor the opinions we have formed.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><b><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">Respective responsibilities of directors and auditor</span></b><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">As explained more fully in the Statement of Directors'\nResponsibilities, the directors are<a></a> responsible for the\npreparation of the financial statements and for being satisfied that<a></a> they give a true and fair view.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>Our responsibility is to audit and express an\nopinion on<a></a> the financial statements in accordance with\napplicable law and International Standards on<a></a> Auditing (UK\nand Ireland).<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>Those standards require us\nto comply with the Auditing<a></a> Practices Board's Ethical\nStandards for Auditors.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><b><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">Scope of the audit of the financial statements</span></b><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">An audit involves obtaining evidence about the amounts and\ndisclosures in the financial<a></a> statements sufficient to give\nreasonable assurance that the financial statements are free<a></a>\nfrom material misstatement, whether caused by fraud or error.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>This includes an assessment<a></a>\nof: whether the accounting policies are appropriate to the company's\ncircumstances and have<a></a> been consistently applied and\nadequately disclosed; the reasonableness of significant<a></a>\naccounting estimates made by the directors; and the overall presentation of the\nfinancial<a></a> statements.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\"> \n</span>In addition, we read all the financial and non-financial information in\nthe<a></a> annual report to identify material inconsistencies with\nthe audited financial statements. If we become aware of any apparent material\nmisstatements or inconsistencies we consider<a></a> the\nimplications for our report.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><b><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">Opinion on financial statements</span></b><span style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Investment\nproperties are revalued annually and in accordance with SSAP 19 (Accounting for\nInvestment Properties) no provision is made for depreciation. This departure\nfrom the requirements of the statutory accounting rules, which requires all\nproperties to be depreciated is, in the opinion of the directors, necessary for\nthe accounts to show a true and fair view. Depreciation is only one of the\nfactors reflected in the annual valuation and the amount attributable to this\nfactor is not capable of being separately identified or quantified. Surpluses\nor deficits are transferred to the revaluation reserve, unless a deficit\nexceeds previous surpluses recognised on the same property, in which case the\nexcess is charged to the profit and loss account.</span></p></div><div></div><div><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-ansi-language:EN-GB;&#xD;&#xA;mso-fareast-language:EN-GB;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA\"><br /></span></div><div></div><div class=\"WordSection11\"><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Development\nproperties</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Properties\nunder development or held for development, comprising leasehold<a></a>\nbuildings and freehold land, are held at cost, subject to provision for\ndiminution in value.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Properties\noccupied by group companies are depreciated over four years.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Investments</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Investments\nin subsidiaries are stated at cost less any provision for impairment.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Trade\nand other debtors</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Debtors\nare recognised initially at fair value.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\"> \n</span>A provision for impairment is established where there is objective\nevidence that the company will not be able to collect all amounts due according\nto the original terms of the debtor concerned.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Trade\nand other creditors</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Trade\nand other creditors are stated at cost.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Debt</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Debt\ninstruments are stated initially at the amount of the net proceeds. The finance\ncosts of such debt instruments are allocated to periods over the term of the\ndebt at a constant rate on the carrying amount. The carrying amount is\nincreased by the finance cost in respect of the reporting period and reduced by\npayments made in respect of the debt of that period. Finance costs are charged\nto the profit and loss account.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Taxation</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Current\ntax is provided at amounts expected to be paid or recovered using the tax rates\nand laws that have been enacted or substantively enacted at the balance sheet\ndate. </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Deferred\ntax assets and liabilities arise from timing differences between the recognition\nof gains and losses in the financial statements and their recognition in the\ncorporation tax return.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Under\nFRS 19 deferred tax is recognised in respect of all timing differences that\nhave originated but not reversed at the balance sheet date where transactions\nor events that result in an obligation to pay more tax in the future or a right\nto pay less tax in the future have occurred at the balance sheet date.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>A net deferred tax asset is regarded as\nrecoverable and therefore recognised only when, on the basis of all available\nevidence, it can be regarded as more likely than not that there will be\nsuitable taxable profits from which the future reversal of the underlying\ntiming differences can be deducted.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Deferred\ntax is not recognised when fixed assets are revalued unless by the balance\nsheet date there is a binding agreement to sell the revalued assets and the\ngain or loss expected to arise on sale has been recognised in the financial\nstatements.</span></p></div><div></div><div><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-ansi-language:EN-GB;&#xD;&#xA;mso-fareast-language:EN-GB;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA\"><br /></span></div><div></div><div class=\"WordSection12\"><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Deferred\ntax is measured on a discounted basis to reflect the time value of money over\nthe period between the balance sheet date and the dates on which it is estimated\nthat the timing differences will reverse, or where the timing differences are\nnot expected to reverse, a period not exceeding 50 years.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>Discount rates of 0.2% to 2.3% have been\nadopted reflecting the post-tax yield to maturity that can be obtained on\ngovernment bonds with similar maturity dates and currencies to those of the\ndeferred tax assets or liabilities.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><a></a><b><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">2.</span></b><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">     </span><b>OPERATING\nPROFIT/(LOSS)</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Operating\nprofit/(loss) is stated after charging:</span></p><table
